<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a> (652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ванна.html>ва́нну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>prinimáju</b> vánnu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m taking a bath</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> ekzámen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to examine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to admit, to accept
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>при́мем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́нов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My <b>prímem</b> nóvyx člénov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We’ll accept new members</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to accept an offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to receive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>госте́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> gostéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">receive visitors</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радиоволна.html>радиово́лны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> radiovólny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">receive radiowaves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assume</li></ol>

***приниматься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ться</a> (3575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinimátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start doing something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приму́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:университетский.html>университе́тской</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мме</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Závtra <b>primúsʹ</b> čitátʹ knígi po universitétskoj prográmme.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Tomorrow I'll start reading books on the university program.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take root
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмо́трим</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>при́мутся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:саженец.html>са́женцы</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Posmótrim, <b>prímutsja</b> li sážency.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's see if the seedlings will take root.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:норовить.html>норови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">norovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***приносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приноси́ть</a> (1888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring (by foot), to fetch</li>
<li>to yield, to bear</li>
<li>to offer <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">apologies, thanks, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приносить.html>приношу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:извинение.html>извине́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязываться.html>обязу́юсь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незаконченный.html>незако́нченную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Prinošú</b> svoí izvinénija i objazújusʹ provestí nezakónčennuju rabótu v udóbnoje dlja vas vrémja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I apologize and I am committing to do the unfinished work at your convenience.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***принтер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a> (18324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">printer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príntɛr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтеров</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">при́нтерный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> printer <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device that prints images and text on paper</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тал</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neisprávnyj <b>príntɛr</b> tólʹko porvál bumágu i ničevó ne pečátal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The broken <b>printer</b> only tore the paper apart and didn't print anything.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<table class="morfotable ru" style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse; max-width:300px;" cellpadding="3" rules="all">

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принудительный.html>принуди́тельный</a> (13705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>прину́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinúditʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to force, to compel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудительный.html>принуди́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinudítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>forced, coercive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудительный.html>принуди́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prinudítelʹnyje rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">forced labor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принудительный.html>принуди́тельные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinudítelʹnyje</b> méry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">coercive measures</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> forced <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by mechanical means</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принудительный.html>принуди́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вентиляция.html>вентиля́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinudítelʹnaja</b> ventiljácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">forced ventilation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***принудить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>прину́дить</a> (12294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>прину́дить</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>принуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinúditʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принуждать.html>принужда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to force, to compel, to coerce</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>принуди́ть</a></b> with ending stress is common but considered substandard.</li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принуждённый.html>принуждённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinuždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принудить.html>прину́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinúditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принц.html>принц</a> (2817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Prinz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">prince</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">princeps</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">first head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">primus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">first</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">capio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally, "one who takes the first part".

***принцип.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нцип</a> (1221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нцип</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príncip</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нципа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нципы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принцип.html>при́нципов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>principle (fundamental assumption)

***принципиальность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принципиальность.html>принципиа́льность</a> (19624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принципиальный.html>принципиа́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">principiálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***принять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a> (446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ванна.html>ва́нну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>prinimáju</b> vánnu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m taking a bath</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душ</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinjátʹ</b> duš</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to take</b> a shower</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to admit, to accept
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>при́мем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>чле́нов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My <b>prímem</b> nóvyx člénov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We’ll accept new members</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to accept an offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to receive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>госте́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prinimátʹ</b> gostéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">receive visitors</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assume</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прия́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prijátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́ться</a> (1075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prinjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start doing (something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>prinjálsja</b> čitátʹ knígi.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He started reading books.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take root
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саженец.html>са́женцы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приняться.html>приня́лись</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sážency býstro <b>prinjálisʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The seedlings have quickly taken root.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Данные облигации могли <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">приобретаться</span> только лицами, состоящими в профессиональном или пенсионном фонде, созданном в соответствии с законом 1962 года «О налогообложении лиц, работающих не по найму, при их выходе на пенсию». </span></li>
